        <title>Rango - Rotten Tomatoes</title>
        <meta name="description" content="A chameleon (Johnny Depp) who has lived as a sheltered family pet finds himself in the grip of an identity crisis. Rango wonders how to stand out when it is his nature to blend in. When he accidentally winds up in a frontier town called Dirt, he takes the first step on a transformational journey as the town's new sheriff. Though at first Rango only role-plays, a series of thrilling situations and outrageous encounters forces him to become a real hero.">

    <section id="what-to-know" class="what-to-know panel-rt panel-box">
        <h2 class=" panel-heading what-to-know__header">What to know</h2>
        <div class="what-to-know__body">
            <section>
                <h3 class="what-to-know__section-title">
                    <score-icon-critic
                        size="tiny"
                        percentage="hide"
                        state="certified-fresh"
                        style="display: inline-block"
                    ></score-icon-critic>
                    <span class="what-to-know__section-title--text">critics consensus</span>
                </h3>
                <p class="what-to-know__section-body">
                    <span data-qa="critics-consensus"><em>Rango</em> is a smart, giddily creative burst of beautifully animated entertainment, and Johnny Depp gives a colorful vocal performance as a household pet in an unfamiliar world.</span>

    <script>
        var mps = mps || {};
        mps._queue = mps._queue || {};
        mps._queue.gptloaded = mps._queue.gptloaded || [];
        mps._queue.adload = mps._queue.adload || [];

        mps._queue.gptloaded.push(function() {
            if (mps.getResponsiveSet() =='0') { //MOBILE
                mps.insertAd('#interscroller_ad','interscroller');
            }
        });
        mps._queue.adload.push(function(eo) {
            if (eo._mps._slot === 'interscroller' && eo.isEmpty) {
                document.querySelector('.mobile-interscroller').classList.add('isEmpty');
            }
        });
    </script>

<section id="audience_reviews" class="panel panel-rt panel-box" data-qa="audience-reviews">
    <h2 class="panel-heading">Audience Reviews for <em>Rango</em></h2>
    
        
        <div class="sr-only js-clamp-live-region" aria-live="polite"></div>
        <ul class="mop-audience-reviews__reviews-wrap clearfix">
            
            
            
                <li class="mop-audience-reviews__review-item pull-left cl" data-qa="quote-bubble">
                    <div class="mop-audience-reviews__review-quote" data-qa="quote-bubble-review">
                        <div class=" clearfix">
                            
                                <span class="star-display" data-qa="star-display"><span class="star-display__filled "></span><span class="star-display__filled "></span><span class="star-display__filled "></span><span class="star-display__half "></span><span class="star-display__empty"></span></span>
                            
                            <span class="mop-audience-reviews__review--duration">Oct 28, 2017</span>
                        </div>
                        
                        <div class="mop-audience-reviews__review--comment clamp clamp-4 js-clamp">Much better than I expected, Full of some great Entertaining scenes and some funny laughs to be had too, Some if not most of the comedy felt like it would go over the target audiences head as allot of jokes only adults would understand fully but it does have its slapstick moments that the kids will love, The animation was good, I can&#39;t comment on the 3D as I watched the 2D version, With a great voice cast this film can be enjoyed by all the family.</div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="mop-audience-reviews__review--user-wrap">
                        
                            <a href="/user/id/788614323">
                            
                                <span class="mop-audience-reviews__review--user-default"></span>
                            
                            </a>
                        
                        <div class="mop-audience-reviews__review--name-wrap">
                            
                                <a href="/user/id/788614323">
                                    <span class="mop-audience-reviews__review--name">Jamie C</span>
                                </a>
                            
                            
                                <strong class="super-reviewer-badge">Super Reviewer</strong>
                            
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </li>
                
                <li class="mop-audience-reviews__review-item pull-right cr" data-qa="quote-bubble">
                    <div class="mop-audience-reviews__review-quote" data-qa="quote-bubble-review">
                        <div class=" clearfix">
                            
                                <span class="star-display" data-qa="star-display"><span class="star-display__filled "></span><span class="star-display__filled "></span><span class="star-display__filled "></span><span class="star-display__half "></span><span class="star-display__empty"></span></span>
                            
                            <span class="mop-audience-reviews__review--duration">Jan 13, 2014</span>
                        </div>
                        
                        <div class="mop-audience-reviews__review--comment clamp clamp-4 js-clamp">Verbinski&#39;s highly creative 3D reimagining of the western genre is a visual feast to behold, full with twists, action, comedy, dangerous characters and almost all the cherished trademarks that you would have liked to see in the genre. Out of the several 3D animated films that have received high acclaim and appraisal, this one lived up to its own hype more accurately.

&lt;i&gt;Rango&lt;/i&gt;&#39;s influences are primarily spaghetti. It is a positive aspect that it didn&#39;t try to compile the different western styles that can be found between the 30s and the 70s, because it gave the characters, the plot and the style a more polished and focused direction. Even if using Timothy Olyphant to portray Clint Eastwood&#39;s &quot;Man with No Name&quot; is a rather insulting thing to do, this is creativity not at its finest form, but definitely visionary and thoroughly refreshing (with hidden gags that only Spanish speakers may get, heh).

72/100</div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="mop-audience-reviews__review--user-wrap">
                        
                            <a href="/user/id/535433355">
                            
                                <span class="mop-audience-reviews__review--user-default"></span>
                            
                            </a>
                        
                        <div class="mop-audience-reviews__review--name-wrap">
                            
                                <a href="/user/id/535433355">
                                    <span class="mop-audience-reviews__review--name">Edgar C</span>
                                </a>
                            
                            
                                <strong class="super-reviewer-badge">Super Reviewer</strong>
                            
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </li>
                
                <li class="mop-audience-reviews__review-item pull-left cl" data-qa="quote-bubble">
                    <div class="mop-audience-reviews__review-quote" data-qa="quote-bubble-review">
                        <div class=" clearfix">
                            
                                <span class="star-display" data-qa="star-display"><span class="star-display__filled "></span><span class="star-display__filled "></span><span class="star-display__filled "></span><span class="star-display__half "></span><span class="star-display__empty"></span></span>
                            
                            <span class="mop-audience-reviews__review--duration">Nov 02, 2013</span>
                        </div>
                        
                        <div class="mop-audience-reviews__review--comment clamp clamp-4 js-clamp">This film is a gem. Great story. The film pays homage to movies like Fear and Loathing in Las Vegas, Apocalypse Now, and Clint Eastwood&#39;s The Man with No Name trilogy, just to name a few. The film is also hilarious.

Johnny Depp shines here. I thought this film was much better than his Lone Ranger film. All the other voice actors do a great job in their roles.

I definitely recommend this film.</div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="mop-audience-reviews__review--user-wrap">
                        
                            <a href="/user/id/460385224">
                            
                                <span class="mop-audience-reviews__review--user-default"></span>
                            
                            </a>
                        
                        <div class="mop-audience-reviews__review--name-wrap">
                            
                                <a href="/user/id/460385224">
                                    <span class="mop-audience-reviews__review--name">Sol C</span>
                                </a>
                            
                            
                                <strong class="super-reviewer-badge">Super Reviewer</strong>
                            
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </li>
                
                <li class="mop-audience-reviews__review-item pull-right cr" data-qa="quote-bubble">
